----------------------------------------

(7) QDPOrderProof (EQUIVALENT)
We use the reduction pair processor [LPAR04,JAR06].


The following pairs can be oriented strictly and are deleted.

   2^1(4(4(2(1(1(4(1(0(1(2(1(0(1(4(0(1(1(1(0(x1)))))))))))))))))))) -> 2^1(1(4(4(x1))))
